`ticks,~`even~`tick~`that~`might~`not~`generate~`you~`a~`shard~`(below~`70%)~J~JsoulShard_fragCounter~`=~`true~`--~`show~`the~`amount~`of~`fragments~`you~`have~`(true~`-~`on,~`false~`-~`off)~J~JsoulShard_singleDigit~`=~`false~`--~`show~`the~`amount~`of~`fragments~`you~`have~`without~`whole~`shards~`(~`e.g.~`6)~J~JsoulShard_pointForm~`=~`false~`--~`show~`the~`amount~`of~`fragments~`you~`have~`in~`demical~`form~`(~`e.g.~`3.6)~J~J--------------------~J--~`Colour~`Options~`--~J--------------------~J~J--~`You~`can~`change~`the~`colours~`of~`each~`of~`the~`bars~`by~`changing~`the~`colours~`inside~`of~`the~`weak~`auras~`default~`settings.~`~J--~`The~`prediction~`colour~`is~`the~`colour~`in~`the~`animations~`tab~J~J--------------------~J--~`How~`Doom~`works~`--~J--------------------~J~J--~`Doom~`is~`a~`dot,~`it~`ticks~`for~`damage~`at~`the~`end~`of~`it's~`duration.~`~J--~`Doom~`can~`partially~`tick~`if~`it's~`doesn't~`tick~`for~`it's~`full~`tickrate.~`~J--~`If~`doom~`is~`going~`to~`fall~`off~`before~`reaching~`it's~`full~`tick~`duration,~`the~`tick~`will~`happen~`at~`the~`end~`of~`Doom's~`duration~`unless~`doom~`is~`refreshed.~`Then~`the~`current~`tick~`will~`take~`how~`ever~`much~`more~`time~`it~`needs~`from~`the~`refresh~`to~`fully~`tick~J--~`Doom's~`pandemic~`window~`is~`based~`on~`your~`current~`haste~`(it's~`current~`tickrate)~J--~`Shard~`generation~`is~`based~`on~`how~`much~`doom~`ticked,~`vs~`it's~`tickrate.~`~J--~`Doom~`snapshots~`haste~`on~`cast,~`but~`the~`hasted~`interval~`is~`only~`calculated,~`from~`the~`next~`tick.~J~J--~`Examples--~J~J--~`Short~`->~`Long~`|~`(High~`Haste~`->~`Low~`Haste)~J~J--~`Let's~`assume~`that~`you~`cast~`doom,~`with~`haste~`such~`that~`it's~`tickrate~`is~`10~`seconds.~`~J--~`Your~`haste~`when~`you~`casted~`the~`Doom,~`has~`now~`snapshotted~`it's~`tickrate~`(10~`seconds).~J--~`If~`your~`haste~`effects~`now~`fall~`off,~`such~`that~`Doom's~`tickrate~`is~`now~`20~`seconds~`(Doom's~`pandemic~`is~`now~`6~`seconds).~J--~`Assume~`that~`you~`now~`refresh~`doom~`at~`4~`seconds~`remaining,~`bringing~`it's~`duration~`up~`to~`24~`seconds.~J--~`Doom~`will~`then~`tick~`4~`seconds~`after~`the~`refresh~`at~`20~`seconds,~`for~`a~`full~`tick.~J--~`The~`next~`doom~`tick~`then~`starts,~`snapshotting~`the~`lest~`refresh's~`haste~`as~`it's~`tickrate.~`~J~J--~`Long~`->~`Short~`|~`(Long~`Haste~`->~`High~`Haste)~J~J--~`Let's~`say~`that~`you~`opened~`with~`Hand~`of~`Gul'dan~`(before~`your~`haste~`procs~`and~`Bloodlust).~`Applying~`a~`Doom~`with~`a~`tickrate~`of~`20~`seconds~`(snapshotting~`your~`haste).~J--~`Now~`you~`gain~`some~`haste,~`through~`the~`effects~`of~`Bloodlust~`and~`whispers,~`and~`Doom's~`tickrate~`is~`brought~`down~`to~`10~`seconds.~J--~`While~`under~`the~`haste~`effects,~`you~`refresh~`doom~`at~`5~`seconds.~`Bringing~`the~`duration~`down~`to~`13~`seconds~`(10~`+~`10*0.3),~`because~`it's~`current~`pandemic~`is~`3~`seconds~J--~`You've~`now~`brought~`the~`duration~`of~`a~`Doom,~`with~`the~`tickrate~`of~`20~`seconds,~`down~`to~`13~`seconds.~J--~`You~`will~`get~`a~`tick~`at~`the~`end~`of~`dooms~`duration,~`that~`will~`deal~`65%~`damage~`(13/20)~`and~`have~`a~`65%~`change~`to~`generate~`a~`shard.~`~J~J--~`Extended~`ticklength~`--~J~J--~`Let's~`imagine~`a~`situation~`in~`which~`you~`refresh~`a~`short~`doom,~`with~`a~`long~`duration~`above~`it's~`pandemic~`threshold.~J--~`For~`simplicity~`we'll~`keep~`the~`ticks~`at~`10~`and~`20~`respectively.~J--~`You~`cast~`Doom~`to~`start~`the~`fight.~`Then~`refresh~`it~`with~`Hand~`of~`Gul'dan~`when~`it~`has~`9~`seconds~`remaining~`(1~`seconds~`after~`you~`applied~`it).~J--~`This~`brings~`the~`duration~`up~`to~`26~`seconds~`(20~`+~`0.3*20).~`~J--~`Doom~`will~`tick~`at~`17~`seconds~`remaining~`(9~`seconds~`after~`the~`refresh),~`snapshotting~`the~`next~`hasted~`interval~`with~`the~`last~`refreshed~`tickrate~`(20~`seconds)~J--~`Following~`the~`logic~`provided,~`Doom~`should~`partially~`tick~`at~`the~`end~`of~`it's~`duration~`for~`85%~`damage,~`and~`an~`85%~`chance~`to~`generate~`a~`shard.~J--~`Now's~`assume~`that~`you~`refresh~`Doom~`before~`it~`expires~`at~`3~`seconds~`remaining,~`pushing~`doom's~`duration~`to~`23~`seconds~`(20~`+~`3).~J--~`Doom~`now~`has~`enough~`time~`to~`make~`a~`full~`tick,~`so~`the~`nexttick~`will~`get~`pushed~`back~`from~`the~`time~`at~`which~`it~`would~`have~`expired~`to~`6~`seconds~`after~`the~`refresh~`(17~`seconds~`remaning)~`~J~J---------------------~J--~`Shard~`Cost~`Info~`--~J---------------------~JSSB_CostInfo~`=~`{~J~`~`~`~`[30108]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Unstable~`Affliction~J~`~`~`~`[27243]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Seed~`of~`Corruption~J~`~`~`~`[116858]~`=~`2,~`~`--~`Chaos~`Bolt~J~`~`~`~`[5740]~`=~`3,~`~`--~`Rain~`of~`Fire~J~`~`~`~`[18540]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Summon~`Doomguard~J~`~`~`~`[688]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Summon~`Imp~J~`~`~`~`[1122]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Summon~`Infernal~J~`~`~`~`[691]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Summon~`Felhunter~J~`~`~`~`[712]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Summon~`Succubus~J~`~`~`~`[697]~`=~`1,~`~`--~`Summon~`Voidwalker~J~`~`~`~`[30146]~`=~`1~`~`--~`Summon~`Felguard~J}~J~J~J--~`Hex~`to~`RGB~`--~J~JsoulShard_hextorgb~`=~`function(hex)~J~`~`~`~`hex~`=~`hex:gsub("#","")~J~`~`~`~`return~`tonumber("0x"..hex:sub(1,2))/255,~`tonumber("0x"..hex:sub(3,4))/255,~`tonumber("0x"..hex:sub(5,6))/255~Jend~J~J~J~J~J~J^Sdo_custom^B^t^t^SnumTriggers^N2^t^N4^T^SyOffset^N46^SregionType^Saurabar^Sanimation^T^Smain^T^Sscalex^N1^Sx^N0^Sduration^S0^Sy^N0^ScolorA^N1^Sscaley^N1^ScolorFunc^Sfunction(progress,~`r1,~`g1,~`b1,~`a1,~`r2,~`g2,~`b2,~`a2)~J~`~`~`~`~J~`~`~`~`local~`red,~`green,~`blue,~`alpha~`=~`1,~`1,~`1,~`1~J~`~`~`~`local~`specID~`=~`GetSpecialization()~J~`~`~`~`local~`ssCount~`=~`UnitPower("player",~`SPELL_POWER_SOUL_SHARDS,~`false);~J~`~`~`~`local~`fragCount~`=~`UnitPower("player",~`SPELL_POWER_SOUL_SHARDS,~`true);~J~`~`~`~`local~`castingInfo~`=~`UnitCastingInfo("player")~J~`~`~`~`local~`currentSpell~`=~`UnitCastingInfo('player');~J~`~`~`~`local~`currentChannel~`=~`UnitChannelInfo('player');~J~`~`~`~`local~`colour~`=~`soulShard_~J~`~`~`~`if~`soulShard_castPrediction~
